<script type="text/javascript">
var CartPerf = (function() {
  var _hasUedata = (typeof uet == 'function');
  var _startedLoading = false;

  var loading = function() {
    if (!_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('cb');
    }
    _startedLoading = true;
  };

  var aboveTheFoldLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('af');
    }
  };

  var functionalLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('fn');
    }
  };

  var criticalFeatureLoaded = function() {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('cf');
    }
  };

  var x1Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x1');
    }
  }

  var _isReportingEvents = function() {
    return _hasUedata;
  };

  var _hasUEForAJAXRequest = (typeof ues == 'function') && (typeof uex == 'function');
  var _actionNumber = 0;
  var _scope = "cart-ajax";

  var getScope = function() {
    return _scope;
  }

  var resetUEForAJAXRequest = function() {
    _actionNumber++;
    _scope = "cart-ajax-" + _actionNumber;
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("tc", _scope);         // set time-of-click
      ues("ctb", _scope, "1");   // set ctb flag
    }
  }

  // set start time
  var setStartTimeForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      ues("t0", _scope, new Date());
    }
  }

  // set request ID
  var setIDForAJAXRequest = function(rid) {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      ues("id", _scope, rid);
    }
  }

  // record the event of critical feature loaded
  var cfLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("cf", _scope);
    }
  }
  
  var atfLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("af", _scope);
    }
  }

  var fnLoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("fn", _scope);
    }
  }

  // record the event of page loaded
  var pageLoadedForAJAXRequest = function(scope) {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      if (scope != null) {
        uex("ld", scope);
      } else {
        uex("ld", _scope);
      }
    }
  }
  
  var x1LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x1", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x2LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x2", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x3LoadedForAJAXRequest = function() {
    if (window.ue && _hasUedata && _hasUEForAJAXRequest) {
      uet("x3", _scope);
    }
  }

  var x2Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x2');
    }
  }

  var x3Loaded = function () {
    if (_startedLoading && _isReportingEvents()) {
      uet('x3');
    }
  }

  loading();

  return {
    aboveTheFoldLoaded:         aboveTheFoldLoaded,
    atfLoadedForAJAXRequest:    atfLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    functionalLoaded:           functionalLoaded,
    fnLoadedForAJAXRequest:     fnLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    cfLoadedForAJAXRequest:     cfLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    criticalFeatureLoaded:      criticalFeatureLoaded,
    x1Loaded:                   x1Loaded,
    getScope:                   getScope,
    pageLoadedForAJAXRequest:   pageLoadedForAJAXRequest,
    resetUEForAJAXRequest:      resetUEForAJAXRequest,
    setIDForAJAXRequest:        setIDForAJAXRequest,
    setStartTimeForAJAXRequest: setStartTimeForAJAXRequest,
    x1LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x1LoadedForAJAXRequest,
    x2Loaded:                   x2Loaded,
    x2LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x2LoadedForAJAXRequest,
    x3Loaded:                   x3Loaded,
    x3LoadedForAJAXRequest:     x3LoadedForAJAXRequest,
  };
})();
</script>

  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , sessionId: opts.sessionId
      , requestId: opts.requestId
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , pageType: opts.pageType
      , language: opts.language
      , customerId: opts.customerId
      , fresh: opts.fresh
      , b2b: opts.b2b
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases
      , fb: issOpts.fallbackFlag
      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , biaWidgetUrl: opts.biaWidgetUrl
      , recentSearchesTreatment: issOpts.recentSearchesTreatment
      , authorSuggestionText: issOpts.authorSuggestionText
      , translatedStringsMap: issOpts.translatedStringsMap
      , biaTitleText: issOpts.biaTitleText
      , biaPurchasedText: issOpts.biaPurchasedText
      , biaViewAllText: issOpts.biaViewAllText
      , biaViewAllManageText: issOpts.biaViewAllManageText
      , biaAndText: issOpts.biaAndText
      , biaManageText: issOpts.biaManageText
      , biaWeblabTreatment: issOpts.biaWeblabTreatment
      , issNavConfig: issOpts.issNavConfig
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
      , removeDeepNodeISS: issOpts.removeDeepNodeISS
      , trendingTreatment: issOpts.trendingTreatment
      , useAPIV2: issOpts.useAPIV2
      , opfSwitch: issOpts.opfSwitch
      , isISSDesktopRefactorEnabled: issOpts.isISSDesktopRefactorEnabled
      , disableNavConfigFetch: issOpts.disableNavConfigFetch
      , isAPICachingDisabled: issOpts.isAPICachingDisabled
      , isInternal: issOpts.isInternal
      , useServiceHighlighting: issOpts.useServiceHighlighting
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

P.register('CartServerSetting', function() {
  return {"requestId":"Y4XCX2AM2XNTGY03YBDE","features":{"enabledVPCValidityMessage":0,"wrapCartPerf":"1","enableCartInstallments":0,"enableBuyNow":"","enabledPseudoPrime":0,"enableAUITabletView":0,"enableFreshCart":"","enableBatching":0,"enableA11yLinks":"","enableMinimumOrderQuantity":1,"FLC":{"zipcodeSupported":""},"enableLoadFullCartAndInfScrollSFL":"1","enablePrimePantry":"","enableLoadAllSavedItems":"","enableWishListIntegration":"","disableUpdateUserQuantityToMOQ":0,"removeFadeInAndOut":"","enableWishListRedesign":0,"enableCollapsedSFL":"","enableAddOnReminder":""},"cartSizeLimit":"50","domain":"prod","view":"Desktop","benefitPriceModalSignupScript":null,"cartQuantityLimit":"100","csrf":{"timeStamp":"1564970967","token":"gBA6GZjDwo0quDOTLq6g0ikok00lYILPN7HBhVsAAAAJAAAAAF1Hj9dyYXcAAAAA","requestID":"Y4XCX2AM2XNTGY03YBDE"}};

<div id="sc-checkout-prefetch" data-assetsprefetchurl="/gp/buy/prefetch/pipeline-assets.html" data-prefetchurl="/gp/cart/checkout-prefetch.html?ie=UTF8&amp;checkAuthentication=1&amp;checkDefaults=1" data-prefetchurlforauthcheck="/gp/remotepagelet/signin/checkout-perf-initiate-and-store.html" class="a-row a-hidden">
  
<script>
P.register('CheckoutPrefetch', function() {
  function convertToQueryString(paramObjects) {
    var params = [];

    for(var i = 0; i < paramObjects.length; i++) {
      var name  = paramObjects[i].name;
      var value = paramObjects[i].value;

      name = (name === 'addressID' ? 'shippingAddressID' : name);

      if (params[name]) continue;

      params.push(name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value));
      params[name] = true;
    }

    return params.join('&');
  }

  function getBuyBoxForm(buyBoxFormId) {
    buyBoxFormId = buyBoxFormId || 'sc-buy-box';

    var buyBoxBlock = document.getElementById(buyBoxFormId);
    if (!buyBoxBlock) return;

    var buyBoxForms = buyBoxBlock.getElementsByTagName('form');
    if (buyBoxForms.length === 0) return;

    return buyBoxForms[0];
  }

  function serializeFormParameters(form) {
    var params = [];

    var selects = form.getElementsByTagName('select');
    for (var i = 0; i < selects.length; i++) {
      if (selects[i].name === 'addressID') {
        var name  = selects[i].name;
        var value = selects[i].options[selects[i].selectedIndex].value;

        params.push({name: name, value: value});
        params[name] = value;
      }
    }

    var inputs = form.getElementsByTagName('input');
    for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
      var input = inputs[i];

      if (input.type !== 'hidden' && input.type !== 'checkbox') continue;

      if (inputs[i].type === 'checkbox' && !inputs[i].checked) continue;

      if (inputs[i].name === 'isToBeGiftWrapped'
        || inputs[i].name === 'addressID'
      ) {
        var name  = inputs[i].name;
        var value = inputs[i].value;

        params.push({name: name, value: value});
        params[name] = value;
      }
    }

    return params;
  }

  function getBuyBoxParameters(buyBoxFormId) {
    var form = getBuyBoxForm(buyBoxFormId);

    return form ? serializeFormParameters(form) : [];
  }

  function getPrefetchData(dataName) {
    var prefetchBlock = document.getElementById('sc-checkout-prefetch');

    return prefetchBlock.getAttribute('data-' + dataName);
  }

  function getAssetsPrefetchUrl() {
    var prefetchBlock = document.getElementById('sc-checkout-prefetch');

    return prefetchBlock.getAttribute('data-assetsprefetchurl');
  }

  function firePrefetchRequest(prefetchUrl) {
    // Why we have to use iframe?
    var iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
    iframe.setAttribute("src", prefetchUrl);
    iframe.setAttribute("style", "width:0px;height:0px;display:none;position:absolute;");
    iframe.setAttribute("name", "checkoutPrefetch;");

    // Why we insert into head?
    if (document.head) {
        document.head.appendChild (iframe);
    } else {
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild (iframe);
    }
  }

  function getInitiateIdInput(buyBoxFormId) {
    var buyBoxForm = getBuyBoxForm(buyBoxFormId);
    if (!buyBoxForm) return;

    var inputs = buyBoxForm.getElementsByTagName('input');
    for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
      if (inputs[i].name === "cartInitiateId") {
        return inputs[i];
      }
    }
  }

  function insertInitiateIdInBuyBox(cartInitiateId, buyBoxFormId) {
    var buyBoxForm = getBuyBoxForm(buyBoxFormId);
    if (!buyBoxForm) return;

    // clear previous one
    var oldInput = getInitiateIdInput(buyBoxFormId);
    if (oldInput) {
      buyBoxForm.removeChild(oldInput);
    }

    // insert a new one
    var input = document.createElement("input");
    input.setAttribute("type", "hidden");
    input.setAttribute("value", cartInitiateId);
    input.setAttribute("name", "cartInitiateId");
    buyBoxForm.appendChild(input);
  }

  function initiateAndStorePurchase() {
    var buyBoxParams = getBuyBoxParameters();

    if (!buyBoxParams['isToBeGiftWrapped']) {
      var cartInitiateId = new Date().getTime();
      var prefetchUrl = getPrefetchData('prefetchurl')
        + "&cartInitiateId=" + cartInitiateId
        + "&" + convertToQueryString(buyBoxParams);

      firePrefetchRequest(prefetchUrl);
      insertInitiateIdInBuyBox(cartInitiateId);
    }

    // Kicking off a parallel fresh prefetch if the fresh PTC button is present
    if (document.getElementById('sc-fresh-buy-box-ptc-button')) {
      var freshBuyBoxParams = getBuyBoxParameters('sc-fresh-buy-box');
      var cartInitiateId = new Date().getTime();
      var freshPrefetchUrl = getPrefetchData('freshprefetchurl');
      if (freshPrefetchUrl) {
        freshPrefetchUrl += "&cartInitiateId=" + cartInitiateId
        + "&" + convertToQueryString(freshBuyBoxParams);

        firePrefetchRequest(freshPrefetchUrl);
        insertInitiateIdInBuyBox(cartInitiateId, 'sc-fresh-buy-box');
      }
    }
  }

  initiateAndStorePurchase();

  P.when('A', 'jQuery').execute('Cart-PrefetchInitiateAndStorePurchase', function(A, $) {
    $(document).delegate('#sc-buy-box form [name=addressID]', 'change', function() {
      initiateAndStorePurchase();
    });

    A.on('sc:ajaxupdate:cf', function() {
      var $thankYouPanel = $('.sc-item-1click-typanel-block-prefetch');
      if ($thankYouPanel.length < 1) {
        initiateAndStorePurchase();
      }
    });

    var savedInitiateId;
    A.on('sc:flcAction:before', function() {
      var input = getInitiateIdInput();
      savedInitiateId = input ? input.value : undefined;
    });

    A.on('sc:flcAction:after', function() {
      if (savedInitiateId) {
        insertInitiateIdInBuyBox(savedInitiateId);
        savedInitiateId = undefined;
      }
    });
  });

  var prefetchingRequiredForMouseover = false;
  var prefetchingDoneForMouseover = false;
  var freshPrefetchingDoneForMouseover = false;
  function initiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover() {
    var buyBoxParams = getBuyBoxParameters();

    if (!buyBoxParams['isToBeGiftWrapped']) {
      var prefetchUrl = getPrefetchData('prefetchurlforauthcheck')
        + "?siteState=" + convertToQueryString(buyBoxParams).replace(/&/g, '|').replace(/=/g, '.')
        + "&onClickPTC=1";

      firePrefetchRequest(prefetchUrl);
    }

    prefetchingDoneForMouseover = true;
  }

  function freshInitiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover() {
    var freshBuyBoxParams = getBuyBoxParameters('sc-fresh-buy-box');

    var freshPrefetchUrl = getPrefetchData('freshprefetchurlforauthcheck');
    if (freshPrefetchUrl) {
      freshPrefetchUrl += "&siteState=" + convertToQueryString(freshBuyBoxParams).replace(/&/g, '|').replace(/=/g, '.')
       + "&onClickPTC=1";

      firePrefetchRequest(freshPrefetchUrl);

      freshPrefetchingDoneForMouseover = true;
    }
  }

  P.when('A', 'jQuery').execute('Cart-ListenEventsForPrefetch', function(A, $) {
    A.on('sc:authportal:check-auth-status', function(data) {
      prefetchingRequiredForMouseover = data.required ? true : false;
    });

    $(document).delegate('#sc-buy-box input[name=proceedToCheckout]', 'mouseenter', function() {
      if (prefetchingRequiredForMouseover && !prefetchingDoneForMouseover) {
        initiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover();
      }
    });

    $(document).delegate('#sc-fresh-buy-box #sc-fresh-buy-box-ptc-button input', 'mouseenter', function() {
      if (prefetchingRequiredForMouseover && !freshPrefetchingDoneForMouseover) {
        freshInitiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover();
      }
    });

    $(document).delegate('#sc-buy-box form [name=addressID]', 'change', function() {
      prefetchingDoneForMouseover = false;
    });

    A.on('sc:ajaxupdate:cf', function() {
      prefetchingRequiredForMouseover = false;
      prefetchingDoneForMouseover = false;
      freshPrefetchingDoneForMouseover = false;
    });
  });

  P.when('ready').execute('Cart-FirePrefetchRequest', function() {
    firePrefetchRequest(getPrefetchData('assetsprefetchurl'));
  });

  return {
    firePrefetchRequest:        firePrefetchRequest,
    convertToQueryString:       convertToQueryString,
    getBuyBoxForm:              getBuyBoxForm,
    serializeFormParameters:    serializeFormParameters,
    getBuyBoxParameters:        getBuyBoxParameters,
    getPrefetchData:            getPrefetchData,
    insertInitiateIdInBuyBox:   insertInitiateIdInBuyBox,
    initiateAndStorePurchase:   initiateAndStorePurchase,
    initiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover: initiateAndStorePurchaseForPTCMouseover
  }
});
</script>

</div>

    var emailchanged = 0;
    var storepipedatahandler;
    var emailchangeattempts = 5;

    function storepipedata() {
        var hframe = jQuery('<iframe src="/gp/buy/prefetch/store-html.html" style="width:0px; height:0px; display:none"></iframe>');
        jQuery('body').append(hframe);

        pipedataattempts++;
        if (pipedataattempts < retrypipedata) {
            storepipedatahandler = setTimeout(storepipedata, 60000);
        }
    }

    jQuery(window).ready(function() {
        if (!emailchanged) {
            storepipedatahandler = setTimeout(storepipedata, 60000);
        }
    });

    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
        jQuery('#ap_email').change(function() {
            if ((emailchanged < emailchangeattempts) && jQuery('#ap_email').val()) {
                jQuery.ajax({url: "/gp/checkoutprefetch/change-email.html", data: {email: jQuery('#ap_email').val()}, headers: {"Cache-Control":"no-cache", "pragma":"no-cache"}});
                if (storepipedatahandler) {
                    clearTimeout(storepipedatahandler);
                }
                emailchanged++;
            }
        });
    });
};
